**stock 1.***Com.a* (general) **स्कन्ध** *m.*

**In the English language it has 37 senses** (Web.), **all connectedat the base with 'trunk of a tree'.**

**In the commercial world it is theshare** (or help)**. स्कन्ध** (Hindi कन्धा)**is useable literally as 'trunk of atree', or figuratively as 'help, assistance'** (कन्धा लगाना),**b** (national debt) **= public debt राष्ट्र-ऋण** *n.,***c** (capital raised in shares by apublic company) अंशपुञ्जी *f.,***d** (goods unsold) **अविक्रीतक** *n.*

Sys- = syn-  
system** *n.* **1.**(a formal scheme, method, mode) **पद्धति** (Const.)**, प्रणाली** *f.***, तन्त्र***n.***2.**(an aggregate

or assemblage of objects united by some form of regular interaction or interdependence) **संहति** *f.***, जाल, तन्त्र** *n.***3.**(the universe) **विश्व***n.***4.**(the body) **देह, शरीर** *n.***5.**(a methodically arranged set) **क्रम** *m.***6.**(a theory) **वाद** *m.***7.***Cryst.* **संहति** *f.* (*see* class)**8.**(of rocks) *Geol.* **तन्त्र** *n.*

**Syzygites = Sporodinia** *Mycol.* **महा-बीजाणु-प्रजाति  
Syzygites megalocarpus = Sporodinia grandis सामान्य महाबीजाणु** (*megalo-* महा-, *-carpus*

'spore' बीजाणु)

**syzygy 1.***Astron.* **विसंयुति** *f.* (the ancient word ग्रहयुतिisinappropriate, as the moon is not a ग्रह.

विसंयुति is better as it includes both वियुति and संयुति), **2.***Zool.* **संमेल** *m.*
